[Kendrick_Lamar / Public image]
Lamar maintains a low public profile, [ 1 ] and is known to be reserved. He is reluctant to publicly discuss his personal life and generally avoids using social media . [ 2 ] [ 3 ] He is also decisive when engaging with mainstream media outlets, although journalists have complimented his " Zen -like" calmness and down to earth personality. [ 4 ] [ 5 ] According to Lamar, he has become "so invested in who I am outside of being famous, sometimes that's all I know. I've always been a person that really didn't dive too headfirst into wanting and needing attention. I mean, we all love attention, but for me, I don't necessarily adore it." [ 6 ] His lyrics have been a topic of media scrutiny, leading to both praise and controversy. [ 7 ] [ 8 ] [ 9 ]

Since the release of Good Kid, M.A.A.D City , some media outlets have described Lamar as the "modern hip hop messiah ". [ 10 ] Some critics dislike his "grating" political infusions, [ 11 ] causing him to be viewed as having a savior complex . [ 12 ] [ 13 ] He has previously likened himself to Nelson Mandela . [ 11 ] Lamar's public perception has also been influenced by the various rap feuds he has been involved with. [ 14 ] [ 15 ] Although some journalists declared him the winner of his highly publicized conflict with Drake , [ 16 ] some felt that his victory was pyrrhic due to the severity of accusations introduced and the spread of online misinformation . [ 17 ] [ 18 ] Lamar has been praised for anti-racism activism, [ 19 ] but has also been labelled as exclusionary towards mixed-race individuals; [ 20 ] Michael Eric Dyson has called him a member of the "cults of pure identity that police the boundaries of Blackness like a rogue and racist cop". [ 21 ] Lamar has also been praised for feminist activism, but criticised for collaborating with abusers of women. [ 22 ] [ 23 ] Some magazines have called " Humble " a feminist song, [ 24 ] although the University of Melbourne 's Lauren Rosewarne criticised his use of the word "bitch" forty times on the song and suggested that he centred male preferences over female preferences. [ 25 ] In view of his social activism, Lamar has been criticised for his silence on atrocities in Palestine and Sudan . [ 26 ]

Lamar has declared himself to be the "greatest rapper alive" due to his personal connection to hip hop. [ 27 ] "I'm not doing it to have a good song, or one good rap, or a good hook , or a good bridge ," he explained to Zane Lowe . "I want to keep doing it every time, period. And to do it every time, you have to challenge yourself and you have to confirm to yourself—not anybody else, confirm to yourself that you're the best, period. [...] That's my drive and that's my hunger, I will always have." [ 28 ]

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Kendrick_Lamar / Personal life]
Lamar announced his engagement to esthetician Whitney Alford, his high school sweetheart , in April 2015. [ 1 ] [ 2 ] Although they keep their relationship private, [ 3 ] Lamar admitted that he suffered a sexual addiction and cheated on Alford multiple times. [ 4 ] Alford contributed background vocals on select tracks from To Pimp a Butterfly (2015), [ 5 ] and was the primary narrator on Mr. Morale & the Big Steppers (2022). [ 6 ] The couple welcomed their first child, a daughter on July 26, 2019. [ 7 ] [ 8 ] They used the cover art for Mr. Morale & the Big Steppers to announce the birth of their second child, a son. [ 9 ] [ 10 ]

Lamar's cousin, Carl Duckworth, goes by the name Karni Ben Israel and belongs to a Hebrew Israelite group in New York City . [ 11 ] On " Yah " Lamar raps: "I'm a Israelite, don't call me black no mo'". [ 12 ]

Lamar is a teetotaler [ 13 ] and lives a drug-free lifestyle. [ 14 ] During October 2012, he recalled once trying marijuana, where the blunt had been laced with Phencyclidine (PCP), and he has not used any drugs since. [ 13 ] In an interview with Starz , Lamar stated he asked to play a drug abuser on the TV series Power , saying Laces was "just a character that I know. I know so well, just growing up in Compton. You grow this type of love for them, you know, in a weird way. You know, you don't want to see nothing happen to them, but you know he's dangerous." [ 15 ]

Lamar is an avid fan of the Los Angeles Dodgers of the MLB, [ 16 ] the Los Angeles Lakers of the NBA, [ 17 ] and the Los Angeles Rams of the NFL. [ 18 ] In 2024, he released a track entitled " Dodger Blue " as a reference to the effect of the team's colors in the city's culture on his album GNX . [ 19 ] [ 20 ]

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Kendrick_Lamar / Other ventures]
Lamar has been described as an "authentic" businessman who takes "calculated steps to establish his brand from the ground-up" and leaves nothing to chance. [ 1 ] He approaches traditional album rollouts with an unorthodox method, using Easter eggs and leaving cryptic messages. [ 2 ] Before releasing a studio album, Lamar shares a promotional single taken from "The Heart", forming a timestamp song series designed to "observe the beating pulse behind his music." [ 3 ] The vulnerable themes explored on the non-album singles have strengthened his relationship with his "inquisitive" fanbase known as Kenfolk. [ 3 ] [ 4 ] His real estate portfolio includes properties in California and New York . [ 5 ] [ 6 ] In 2011, Lamar crafted an original song with record producer Nosaj Thing to promote Microsoft 's Windows Phone in 2011. [ 7 ] He starred alongside DJ Calvin Harris and singer Ellie Goulding in a marketing campaign for Bacardi in 2014. [ 8 ]

As a minority shareholder of TDE, Lamar was set to serve as the executive producer for the label's film division. [ 9 ] He partnered with American Express on advertising campaigns for Art Basel and Small Business Saturday , [ 10 ] and is an angel investor of the music creation platform EngineEars. [ 11 ] Lamar has also partnered with several fashion designers and outlets. As a brand ambassador , he was involved with designing sneakers for Reebok and Nike, Inc. [ 12 ] [ 13 ] He developed working relationships with Grace Wales Bonner and Martine Rose ; through their respective eponymous brands, they have dressed him for several public events. [ 14 ] For her Autumn/Winter 2023 collection, Twilight Reverie, Lamar worked with Bonner to create the show's soundtrack with Sampha and Duval Timothy . [ 15 ] [ 16 ] Through PGLang, he composed the score and co-designed the stage for Chanel 's Spring/Summer 2024 haute couture collection. [ 17 ]

A supporter of the Black Lives Matter movement, Lamar is a vocal advocate for racial equality . [ 18 ] In 2012, he commended Frank Ocean for coming out . [ 19 ] Lamar developed a strong friendship with former US president Barack Obama , having worked on a promotional video for Obama's My Brother's Keeper initiative. [ 20 ] [ 21 ] He was critical of Donald Trump's first presidency and the U.S. Supreme Court 's landmark decision to overturn Roe v. Wade . [ 22 ] [ 23 ]

Lamar has headlined charity concerts benefitting local and international non-profit organizations . [ 24 ] [ 25 ] He donated to the American Red Cross in November 2012 to support victims of Hurricane Sandy . [ 26 ] In December 2013, Lamar donated $50,000 to his alma mater, Centennial High School, in support of its music department. [ 27 ] He embarked on a small concert tour in 2014, and donated all of the revenue to Habitat for Humanity and his hometown. [ 28 ] In July 2017, Lamar purchased a wheelchair-accessible van for a quadriplegic fan. [ 29 ] [ 30 ] He has regularly performed at TDE's annual holiday toy drive at Nickerson Gardens , [ 31 ] [ 32 ] and organizes his own toy drive in Compton. [ 33 ] He joined a peace walk in June 2020 to protest against the murder of George Floyd and the killing of Breonna Taylor . [ 34 ] [ 35 ] In June 2024, Lamar spearheaded a $200,000 donation to 20 charities and community initiatives based in Los Angeles . [ 36 ]

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Kendrick_Lamar / Entrepreneurship]
Lamar has been described as an "authentic" businessman who takes "calculated steps to establish his brand from the ground-up" and leaves nothing to chance. [ 1 ] He approaches traditional album rollouts with an unorthodox method, using Easter eggs and leaving cryptic messages. [ 2 ] Before releasing a studio album, Lamar shares a promotional single taken from "The Heart", forming a timestamp song series designed to "observe the beating pulse behind his music." [ 3 ] The vulnerable themes explored on the non-album singles have strengthened his relationship with his "inquisitive" fanbase known as Kenfolk. [ 3 ] [ 4 ] His real estate portfolio includes properties in California and New York . [ 5 ] [ 6 ] In 2011, Lamar crafted an original song with record producer Nosaj Thing to promote Microsoft 's Windows Phone in 2011. [ 7 ] He starred alongside DJ Calvin Harris and singer Ellie Goulding in a marketing campaign for Bacardi in 2014. [ 8 ]

As a minority shareholder of TDE, Lamar was set to serve as the executive producer for the label's film division. [ 9 ] He partnered with American Express on advertising campaigns for Art Basel and Small Business Saturday , [ 10 ] and is an angel investor of the music creation platform EngineEars. [ 11 ] Lamar has also partnered with several fashion designers and outlets. As a brand ambassador , he was involved with designing sneakers for Reebok and Nike, Inc. [ 12 ] [ 13 ] He developed working relationships with Grace Wales Bonner and Martine Rose ; through their respective eponymous brands, they have dressed him for several public events. [ 14 ] For her Autumn/Winter 2023 collection, Twilight Reverie, Lamar worked with Bonner to create the show's soundtrack with Sampha and Duval Timothy . [ 15 ] [ 16 ] Through PGLang, he composed the score and co-designed the stage for Chanel 's Spring/Summer 2024 haute couture collection. [ 17 ]

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Kendrick_Lamar / Philanthropy and activism]
A supporter of the Black Lives Matter movement, Lamar is a vocal advocate for racial equality . [ 1 ] In 2012, he commended Frank Ocean for coming out . [ 2 ] Lamar developed a strong friendship with former US president Barack Obama , having worked on a promotional video for Obama's My Brother's Keeper initiative. [ 3 ] [ 4 ] He was critical of Donald Trump's first presidency and the U.S. Supreme Court 's landmark decision to overturn Roe v. Wade . [ 5 ] [ 6 ]

Lamar has headlined charity concerts benefitting local and international non-profit organizations . [ 7 ] [ 8 ] He donated to the American Red Cross in November 2012 to support victims of Hurricane Sandy . [ 9 ] In December 2013, Lamar donated $50,000 to his alma mater, Centennial High School, in support of its music department. [ 10 ] He embarked on a small concert tour in 2014, and donated all of the revenue to Habitat for Humanity and his hometown. [ 11 ] In July 2017, Lamar purchased a wheelchair-accessible van for a quadriplegic fan. [ 12 ] [ 13 ] He has regularly performed at TDE's annual holiday toy drive at Nickerson Gardens , [ 14 ] [ 15 ] and organizes his own toy drive in Compton. [ 16 ] He joined a peace walk in June 2020 to protest against the murder of George Floyd and the killing of Breonna Taylor . [ 17 ] [ 18 ] In June 2024, Lamar spearheaded a $200,000 donation to 20 charities and community initiatives based in Los Angeles . [ 19 ]

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Kendrick_Lamar / Achievements]
Throughout his career, Lamar has won 27 Grammy Awards ( the most by a rapper in history ), [ 1 ] [ 2 ] [ 3 ] two Primetime Emmy Awards , [ 4 ] five American Music Awards , [ 5 ] 37 BET Hip Hop Awards (the most won by any artist), [ 6 ] 11 MTV Video Music Awards (including two Video of the Year wins), [ 7 ] 7 Billboard Music Awards , [ 8 ] and a Brit Award . [ 9 ] As a songwriter, he has received nominations for an Academy Award and a Golden Globe Award . [ 10 ] [ 11 ] At the 58th Annual Grammy Awards , Lamar received the most Grammy nominations by a rapper in one night , with 11. [ 12 ] [ 13 ] During the 65th ceremony , he became the first artist from any genre to be nominated for Album of the Year with four consecutive lead studio albums since Billy Joel (1979–1983). [ 14 ]

Lamar has appeared in various power listings. In 2015, he was featured on Ebony ' s Power 100 list that honors leaders within the African American community. [ 15 ] Time included him on its annual list of the 100 most influential people in the world in 2016. [ 16 ] He has appeared on Forbes ' Celebrity 100 ranking (2019), [ 17 ] and its 30 Under 30 list twice in the music category (2014 and 2018). [ 18 ] [ 19 ] Lamar was included twice in Billboard ' s lists of the greatest rappers of all time (2015 and 2023). [ 20 ] [ 21 ] Complex named him the best rapper alive thrice (2013, 2017 and 2024), [ 22 ] [ 23 ] and included him in their list of the 20 best rappers in their 20s thrice (2013, 2015, and 2016). [ 24 ] In May 2015, Lamar was declared a generational icon by the California State Senate for his contributions to music and philanthropy. [ 25 ] He was a grand marshal for the Compton Christmas Parade, [ 26 ] and was presented with the key to the city of his hometown for representing its evolution. [ 27 ] He served as Compton College 's surprise commencement speaker on June 7, 2024. [ 28 ] Lamar is the fifth man to appear solo on the cover of Harper's Bazaar . [ 29 ]

Good Kid, M.A.A.D City , To Pimp a Butterfly , and Damn were featured in Rolling Stone ' s industry-voted ranking of the 500 greatest albums of all time and the 200 greatest hip hop albums of all time. [ 30 ] [ 31 ] Good Kid, M.A.A.D City was additionally featured in the magazine's list of the 100 best debut albums of all time, and was named the greatest concept album ever. [ 32 ] [ 33 ] It was named the seventh greatest album of all time by Apple Music in 2024. [ 34 ] To Pimp a Butterfly was ranked by several publications as one of the greatest albums of the 2010s decade, [ 35 ] while "Alright" was deemed the greatest hip hop song of the streaming era by Spotify . [ 36 ] As of February 2023, it is the top ranked album on the online encyclopedia Rate Your Music . [ 37 ] Damn is the recipient of the 2018 Pulitzer Prize for Music , the first time a musical work outside of the classical and jazz genres was honored. [ 38 ] [ 39 ] Its tour companion , along with the Big Steppers Tour (2022–2024), are two of the highest-grossing hip hop tours of all time. [ 40 ]

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Kendrick_Lamar / Legacy]
Insider Inc. and CNN editors have opined that Lamar is one of the most influential musicians of the 2010s decade , deeming him a paradigm shift in contemporary hip hop and popular culture . [ 1 ] [ 2 ] Throughout the Black Lives Matter movement and events following the 2016 U.S. presidential election , his work has been used as protest anthems . [ 3 ] According to American studies and media scholar William Hoynes, Lamar's progressive elements places him amongst other African American artists and activists who "worked both inside and outside of the mainstream to advance a counterculture that opposes the racist stereotypes being propagated in white-owned media and culture." [ 4 ] Matt Miller of Esquire opined in 2017 that Lamar revived music videos as a form of social commentary. [ 5 ]

Lamar's music has frequently achieved commercial success and consistently garnered critical acclaim as well as support from artists who have paved the way for his advancement. [ 6 ] [ 7 ] His Pulitzer Prize win was considered a sign of the American cultural elite formally recognizing hip hop as a "legitimate artistic medium". [ 8 ] Senior artists such as Nas , [ 9 ] Bruce Springsteen , [ 10 ] Eminem , [ 11 ] Dr. Dre , [ 12 ] Prince , [ 13 ] and Madonna have praised his musicianship. [ 14 ] David Bowie 's final album, Blackstar (2016), was inspired by To Pimp a Butterfly , and its producer Tony Visconti praised Lamar as a "rulebreaker" in the music industry. [ 15 ] [ 16 ] Pharrell Williams called him "one of the greatest writers of our times" and likened him to Bob Dylan . [ 17 ] Lamar has also been cited as a strong influence on the works of various modern artists, [ 18 ] including BTS , [ 19 ] Dua Lipa , [ 20 ] Tyler, the Creator , [ 21 ] Roddy Ricch , [ 22 ] and Rosalía . [ 23 ] Lorde regards him as "the most popular and influential artist in modern music." [ 24 ] A Temple University course on Lamar's life, cultural influences, and legacy began in the fall 2025 semester. [ 25 ] [ 26 ]
