[Taylor_Swift / Videos and filmmaking]
Swift emphasizes visuals as a key creative component of her music. [ 1 ] She established her production company, Taylor Swift Productions , in 2008. [ 2 ] Her directorial debut was the music video for "Mine", co-directed with Roman White , in 2010; [ 3 ] and she developed the concept and treatment for "Mean" in 2011. [ 4 ] For the music videos of the 1989 and Reputation singles, she collaborated extensively with the director Joseph Kahn on eight videos; [ 5 ] among them, she produced "Bad Blood", which won Best Music Video at the Grammy Awards in 2016. [ 6 ] She worked with American Express for the "Blank Space" music video (which Kahn directed) and served as executive producer for the interactive app AMEX Unstaged: Taylor Swift Experience , for which she won a Primetime Emmy Award for Outstanding Interactive Program in 2015. [ 7 ]

Swift has directed 15 of her music videos . [ 8 ] [ 9 ] "The Man" was her first solo directorial work and made her the first female artist to win the MTV Video Music Award for Best Direction . [ 10 ] All Too Well: The Short Film , her filmmaking debut, made her the first artist to win the Grammy Award for Best Music Video as a solo director. [ 11 ] [ 12 ] In June 2023, Swift was invited to the Academy of Motion Picture Arts and Sciences . [ 13 ] She has cited Joseph Kahn, Chloé Zhao , Greta Gerwig , Nora Ephron , Guillermo del Toro , John Cassavetes , and Noah Baumbach as filmmaking influences. [ 1 ] [ 14 ]

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Taylor_Swift / Achievements]
Swift has won 14 Grammy Awards, including a record four Album of the Year wins; [ 1 ] she has also received a record eight nominations for Song of the Year . [ 2 ] Swift has additionally won 12 Country Music Association Awards, [ 3 ] 8 Academy of Country Music Awards, [ 4 ] 2 Brit Awards , [ 5 ] and an Emmy Award . [ 6 ] She is the most-awarded artist of the American Music Awards (40 wins), [ 7 ] the Billboard Music Awards (49), [ 8 ] and the MTV Video Music Awards (30, tied with Beyoncé ). [ 9 ] Swift is the first woman to be honored with the Pinnacle Award by the Country Music Association Awards in 2013 and with the Global Icon Award by the Brit Awards in 2021. [ 10 ] [ 5 ]

At the 2016 BMI Pop Awards , Swift became the first female songwriter to receive an award named after its recipient. [ 11 ] She is the youngest person included on Rolling Stone 's list " The 100 Greatest Songwriters of All Time " (2015) and the youngest female inductee into the Songwriters Hall of Fame (2026). [ 12 ] [ 13 ] She received the Songwriter Icon Award from the National Music Publishers' Association in 2021 and was named the Songwriter-Artist of the Decade by the Nashville Songwriters Association International in 2022. [ 14 ] [ 15 ] Swift was included on The New York Times ' list "The 30 Greatest Living American Songwriters" in 2026—determined by votes from six of its critics and over 250 music experts—and is set to be inducted into the Central Pennsylvania Music Hall of Fame in 2027. [ 16 ] [ 17 ]

The International Federation of the Phonographic Industry (IFPI) has named Swift the Global Recording Artist of the Year a record six times (2014, 2019, 2022–2025). [ 18 ] She is the most-streamed artist of all time on Spotify as of April 2026, [ 19 ] and the highest-grossing touring act of all time , with cumulative revenue at $3.12 billion as of December 2024. [ 20 ] Her chart records include the most number-one albums in the UK and Ireland for a female artist in the 21st century; [ 21 ] [ 22 ] the first artist to occupy the top five of the Australian albums chart , doing so twice, [ 23 ] [ 24 ] and the top 10 positions on the Australian singles chart; [ 25 ] and the most entries, most simultaneous entries, and most number-one entries for a soloist on the Billboard Global 200 . [ 26 ] [ 27 ]

In the US, Swift has sold 116.7 million album units, including 54 million pure sales, as of May 2025. [ 28 ] She is the solo artist with the most Billboard 200 number-one albums (15, tied with Drake ) [ 29 ] [ 30 ] and the most weeks at number one on the chart (98); [ 31 ] the female artist with the most Billboard Hot 100 number-one debuts (8, tied with Ariana Grande ); [ 32 ] [ 33 ] the artist with the most number-one songs on Pop Airplay (15) and Adult Pop Airplay (15, tied with Maroon 5 ); [ 34 ] the first living artist to chart five albums in the top 10 of the Billboard 200; [ 35 ] and the first artist to spend one hundred weeks atop the Billboard Artist 100 . [ 36 ] Swift is the first woman to have both an album and a song receive diamond certifications from the Recording Industry Association of America (RIAA), [ 37 ] and also to have 100 million RIAA-certified album units. [ 38 ] Billboard ranked Swift at number eight on its list "Greatest of All Time Artists" (2019), [ 39 ] number three on "Top Country Artists of the 21st Century" (2025), [ 40 ] number two on " Greatest Pop Stars of the 21st Century " (2024), [ 41 ] and number one on "Top 100 Women Artists of the 21st Century" and "Top Artists of the 21st Century" (both 2025). [ 42 ] [ 43 ]

Swift has appeared in power listings. In 2024, she became the first solo artist to top Billboard 's annual Power 100 ranking of the top music industry executives. [ 44 ] Time included her on its annual list of the 100 most influential people in 2010, 2015, and 2019. [ 45 ] [ 46 ] [ 47 ] Swift was one of the "Silence Breakers" that the magazine spotlighted as Person of the Year in 2017 for speaking up about sexual assault. [ 48 ] In 2023, she became the first individual from the arts to be named Time Person of the Year and the first woman to appear on a Person of the Year cover more than once. [ 49 ] [ 50 ] Swift received an honorary Doctor of Fine Arts degree from New York University and served as its commencement speaker on May 18, 2022. [ 51 ]

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Taylor_Swift / Public image]
Swift is an enduring figure of 21st-century popular culture . [ 1 ] Her career trajectory from a country singer-songwriter to a pop star in the 2000s and 2010s was the subject of extensive commentary. [ 2 ] [ 3 ] Deemed "America's Sweetheart" in her early career, she was described in the press as a "media darling" with a girl-next-door 's polite demeanor and open-hearted conversations. [ 4 ] [ 5 ] Swift displayed a feminine image but refrained from the "aggressively sexualized feminist pop" of her contemporaries, leading publications to comment that her sex appeal was modest, subtle, and sophisticated. [ 2 ] [ 6 ] [ 7 ] The adolescent themes of Swift's music contributed to her status as a teen idol , [ 8 ] [ 9 ] although several feminist authors took issue with her songs about romantic relationships as narrow-minded and detrimental to girls and women, who made up the majority of her fanbase known as Swifties . [ 10 ]

Upon recalibrating her artistry to pop music, Swift has identified as a feminist and achieved a pop icon status. [ 11 ] [ 5 ] In 2013, the author Jody Rosen labelled Swift the "Queen of Pop", citing her popularity that defied traditional boundaries between "genres, eras, demographics, paradigms, trends". [ 2 ] Her feminist public image garnered varied reactions from the public, including praise for her success in a male-dominated music industry as an inspiration for girls and women, and criticism that dismissed her feminist adoption as superficial and self-interested. [ 12 ]

The 2016 dispute with Kanye West bolstered the narrative among Swift's detractors that she was a calculating and manipulative woman despite her sweetheart image, and deepened their feud that has resonated in their respective careers. [ 13 ] [ 14 ] Her artistic reinventions in the 2020s turned her into an acclaimed singer-songwriter. [ 15 ] Buoyed by her enduring pop stardom, she has been recognized as a rare phenomenon that combines the pop star and singer-songwriter archetypes with unprecedented success. [ 16 ] [ 17 ] Swift is a known triskaidekaphile , using the number 13 in her various works. [ 18 ]

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Taylor_Swift / Cultural impact]
Swift is one of the few artists to have consistently sold millions of albums across two decades despite the post- album era decline in record sales. [ 1 ] [ 2 ] Academics and journalists have therefore described her as "the last pop superstar" and "the last great rock star" of the 21st century. [ 3 ] [ 4 ] [ 5 ] Her commercial strategies for albums and concert tickets have earned her a reputation as a savvy businesswoman, [ 6 ] [ 7 ] [ 8 ] and her use of physical album variants and easter eggs have become indicative of music marketing trends. [ 9 ] [ 10 ] The economist Alan Krueger described Swift as an "economic genius". [ 11 ] Billboard has considered her one of the few artists who can simultaneously achieve chart success, critical acclaim, and fan support, and popularize any sound in mainstream music. [ 12 ] [ 13 ]

Swift's success in country music has been credited with popularizing the genre beyond the US and introducing it to adolescent women, a previously ignored demographic. [ 14 ] [ 15 ] [ 16 ] The critic Kelefa Sanneh described her as the biggest country star since Garth Brooks , "and maybe since before him, too". [ 17 ] Swift's guitar performances has resulted in increasing sales of guitars among women, which the media dubbed the "Taylor Swift factor". [ 18 ] [ 19 ] Her transition from country to pop has been credited as the catalyst for poptimism, [ 20 ] and her songwriting and musical transitions have been credited with influencing a new generation of artists. [ 21 ] [ 16 ] [ 22 ]

Swift's enduring popularity, particularly among women, has contributed to her status as a representation of millennials , [ 23 ] or, more broadly, of her generation's zeitgeist . [ 24 ] [ 25 ] Her fanbase has been described by academics and journalists as one of the most loyal and dedicated. [ 26 ] [ 27 ] [ 28 ] Time 's Cady Lang credited Swift's sustained superstardom to her "savvy manipulation of both the industry and [her] personal brand". [ 29 ] According to the popular-culture scholars Mary Fogarty and Gina Arnold , Swift is arguably the singular artist "whose story encapsulates many of the urgent conflicts in early twenty-first-century American culture". [ 30 ] In a 2024 article for The New York Times , Joe Coscarelli wrote that her lasting popularity provoked debates comparing her not only to contemporaries like Drake or Beyoncé, but also to veteran artists like the Beatles , Michael Jackson , Elton John , or Madonna. [ 31 ]

Swift's advocacy for artists' rights and re-recording projects have contributed to industry-wide discourses and reforms. [ 32 ] [ 33 ] [ 34 ] Her artistry and career maneuvers have been the subject of various university courses in literary, cultural, and sociopolitical contexts. [ 35 ] [ 36 ] Swift's legacy has been both embraced and critiqued by groups ranging from feminist and queer communities to far-right and religious organizations, and studied by experts across various fields including musicology, literature, sociology, media theory, linguistics, and culture studies. [ 37 ]

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Taylor_Swift / Wealth and endorsements]
Through her management company, TAS Rights Management, LLC, Swift has filed over 300 trademark applications in the US and holds more than 400 registrations worldwide, as of August 2025 [update] . Her filings include her name "Taylor Swift", her fanbase name "Swifties", album and tour titles, lyrics, slogans, artwork, and her cats' names. [ 1 ] In 2026, Swift filed to trademark her voice and appearance against AI-generated reproductions , following unauthorized uses of her likeness in deepfake pornography and presidential election advertisements. [ 2 ]

Swift was listed by Forbes as the world's highest-paid musician in 2016 and 2019, [ 3 ] [ 4 ] the highest-paid female musician of the 2010s, [ 5 ] and the highest-paid female musician in 2021, 2022, and 2025. [ 6 ] [ 7 ] [ 8 ] In October 2023, it was reported that Swift had become a billionaire . [ 9 ] [ 10 ] She was recognized as the first billionaire "primarily based on her songs and performances", with the majority of her fortune coming from royalties and touring. [ 9 ] As of March 2026, [update] Forbes estimated her net worth at $2 billion, making her the world's richest female musician ; the estimate included a $900 million music catalog and a $100 million real estate portfolio that spans Nashville, New York City, Los Angeles ( Samuel Goldwyn Estate ), and Rhode Island ( High Watch ). [ 9 ] [ 11 ] [ 12 ]

Swift's use of private jets has drawn scrutiny for its carbon emissions . [ 13 ] [ 14 ] In 2023, a spokesperson for Swift stated that she had purchased more than double the required carbon credits to offset all tour travel and personal flights. [ 15 ] In December 2023, Swift's lawyers sent a cease and desist letter to the American programmer Jack Sweeney , who uses publicly available data to track her private jet, alleging stalking and safety risks. [ 16 ] [ 17 ] In February 2024, it was reported that Swift had sold one of her two private jets. [ 18 ]

Swift's album rollouts typically consist of multimedia promotional activities involving corporate tie-ins and product endorsements. [ 19 ] [ 20 ] Target is a long-standing business partner with Swift, offering exclusive physical albums and merchandise. [ 21 ] [ 22 ] In 2008–2011, her albums and tours were promoted with self-designed dolls with Jakks Pacific , fragrances with Elizabeth Arden , clothes with L.E.I. , and holiday cards with American Greetings . [ 21 ] [ 23 ] Her partnership deals also included makeup products for CoverGirl and Cyber-shot cameras for Sony Electronics . [ 21 ] In 2012–2015, she had tie-ins with Starbucks , Keds , Subway , Diet Coke , Walgreens , Walmart , and Papa John's . [ 24 ] [ 25 ] Other partnerships included New York City naming her its tourism ambassador in 2014, [ 26 ] an exclusive Apple Music streaming deal in 2015, [ 27 ] a multi-year AT&T deal in 2016, [ 28 ] a United Parcel Service album distribution deal in 2017, [ 29 ] and a multi-year Capital One deal and a clothing line with Stella McCartney in 2019. [ 30 ] [ 31 ] She became the first global ambassador for Record Store Day in 2022. [ 32 ]

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Taylor_Swift / Social activism]
Swift avoided discussing politics in her early career. [ 1 ] She said that she kept herself as educated as possible but did not want to influence others with her political opinions, [ 2 ] later attributing her reluctance to the 2003 Dixie Chicks controversy and its impact on country musicians, especially women. [ 3 ] Due to her apolitical stance, she was appropriated by the alt-right movement in the US, which sparked controversy. [ 4 ] Swift voted for Barack Obama in the 2008 and 2012 US presidential elections , and for Hillary Clinton in the 2016 election ; she did not publicly endorse Clinton because she believed that the backlash she was facing at the time could make her endorsement harmful to Clinton's likability. [ 5 ]

Since 2018, Swift has been public about her political views and has abandoned her once-apolitical stance. [ 6 ] [ 7 ] She publicly endorsed two Democratic politicians for the 2018 US midterm election , which resulted in headlines about how she finally dissociated herself from the alt-right and conservatives . [ 4 ] In 2020, she urged her fans to check their voter registration ahead of elections, which resulted in 65,000 people registering to vote within one day of her post. [ 8 ] Swift endorsed the Democratic ticket of Joe Biden and Kamala Harris in the 2020 US presidential election , and later endorsed Harris and Tim Walz for the 2024 election . [ 5 ] She has openly criticized President Donald Trump and his policies. [ 7 ] [ 5 ]

A pro-choice feminist, [ 9 ] Swift is a founding signatory of the Time's Up movement against sexual harassment [ 10 ] and has criticized the US Supreme Court 's 2022 decision to end federal abortion rights . [ 11 ] A supporter of LGBTQ rights , [ 12 ] she has donated to GLAAD and the Tennessee Equality Project , [ 13 ] [ 14 ] advocated for the Equality Act , [ 15 ] and performed during WorldPride NYC 2019 at the Stonewall Inn , a gay rights monument. [ 16 ] Swift has spoken up against white supremacy , racism, and police brutality in the US. [ 17 ] [ 9 ] She has donated to March for Our Lives and supported gun control and reform in the US , [ 18 ] donated to the NAACP Legal Defense and Educational Fund and supported the Black Lives Matter movement, [ 19 ] called for the removal of Confederate monuments in Tennessee, [ 20 ] and advocated for Juneteenth to become a national holiday. [ 21 ]

Swift's political engagements have been met with mixed reception: they have provoked further public discussion of political issues and empowered Swifties, but critics have questioned whether her political alignments were strategic in her career. [ 22 ] While some publications have argued that Swift's stardom had a significant impact on political involvement in the US, others have viewed her influence as sizable but overstated. [ 23 ] [ 24 ] According to the popular culture scholar Simone Driessen, her political impact extended beyond the US to Australia and Europe. [ 25 ]

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Taylor_Swift / Philanthropy]
Swift ranked first on DoSomething 's "Gone Good" list in 2012, 2013, 2014, and 2015. [ 1 ] [ 2 ] She received the Star of Compassion from the Tennessee Disaster Services and the Big Help Award from the Nickelodeon Kids' Choice Awards for her "dedication to helping others" and "inspiring others through action". [ 3 ] [ 4 ] Especially early in her career, Swift donated to various relief funds following natural disasters. In 2009, she donated $100,000 to the Red Cross to help the victims of the Iowa flood of 2008 . [ 5 ] The same year, she performed at Sydney's Sound Relief concert, which raised money for those impacted by bushfires and flooding. [ 6 ] In 2011, Swift used a dress rehearsal of her Speak Now tour as a benefit concert for victims of recent tornadoes in the US, raising more than $750,000. [ 7 ] In response to the May 2010 Tennessee floods , she donated $500,000. [ 8 ] In 2009, Swift sang at the BBC 's Children in Need concert and raised £ 13,000 for the cause. [ 9 ] In 2016, she donated $1 million to Louisiana flood relief efforts and $100,000 to the Dolly Parton Fire Fund. [ 10 ] [ 11 ] Swift donated to food banks after Hurricane Harvey struck Houston in 2017. [ 12 ] She donated $1 million to Tennessee tornado relief in 2020 and again in 2023 , [ 13 ] [ 14 ] as well as $5 million to relief efforts after Hurricane Helene and Hurricane Milton in 2024. [ 15 ]

She has also donated to cancer research . As the recipient of the Academy of Country Music 's Entertainer of the Year in 2011, Swift donated $25,000 to St. Jude Children's Research Hospital , Tennessee. [ 16 ] In 2012, she participated in the Stand Up to Cancer telethon, performing the charity single " Ronan ", which she wrote in memory of a four-year-old boy who died of neuroblastoma . [ 17 ] She has also donated $100,000 to the V Foundation for Cancer Research [ 18 ] and $50,000 to the Children's Hospital of Philadelphia . [ 19 ] She has made donations to her fans several times to help cover their medical or academic expenses. [ 20 ] During the COVID-19 pandemic, Swift donated to the World Health Organization and Feeding America [ 21 ] and supported independent record stores. [ 22 ] [ 23 ] She performed " Soon You'll Get Better " on the One World: Together At Home television special, a benefit concert curated by Lady Gaga for Global Citizen to raise funds for the World Health Organization's COVID-19 Solidarity Response Fund . [ 24 ]

Swift is a supporter of the arts. A benefactor of the Nashville Songwriters Hall of Fame , [ 25 ] she has donated $75,000 to Hendersonville High School to help refurbish its auditorium; [ 26 ] $4 million to the Country Music Hall of Fame and Museum in Nashville—the largest donation the museum had received from an artist—to establish the Taylor Swift Education Center, an exhibit and classroom space that opened in 2013; [ 27 ] [ 28 ] and $100,000 to the Nashville Symphony . [ 29 ] In 2012, Swift partnered with Chegg for Good to donate $10,000 to the music departments of six US colleges. [ 30 ]

Swift has also provided one-off donations. She has donated items, including signed guitars and concert tickets, to various charities for auction, among them MusiCares , Global's Make Some Noise , and Rare Impact Fund . [ 31 ] [ 32 ] [ 33 ] In 2007, Swift partnered with the Tennessee Association of Chiefs of Police to launch a campaign to protect children from online predators. [ 34 ] She has also encouraged youth to volunteer in their local communities as part of Global Youth Service Day . [ 35 ] A promoter of children's literacy, Swift has donated money and books to schools across the US. [ 36 ] [ 37 ] In April 2018, Swift donated to the Rape, Abuse & Incest National Network in honor of Sexual Assault Awareness Month . [ 38 ] She also donated to fellow singer-songwriter Kesha to help with her legal battles against Dr. Luke and to actress Mariska Hargitay 's Joyful Heart Foundation . [ 38 ] [ 39 ]

Swift donated the equivalent of tens of thousands of meals to food banks at each stop of the Eras Tour; [ 40 ] she also employed local businesses throughout the tour and gave $197 million in bonus payments to her entire crew. [ 41 ] In February 2024, she donated $100,000 to the family of a woman who died in a shooting at the Kansas City Chiefs' Super Bowl parade . [ 42 ] Swift donated $250,000 to Operation Breakthrough in December 2024; the funds were directed to workforce development, childcare, and early learning programs. [ 43 ] In December 2025, she made donations to eight organizations including MusiCares, Operation Breakthrough, Feeding America, and the American Heart Association . [ 44 ] [ 45 ]
