--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Billie_Eilish / Other ventures]
Much of the media attention surrounding Eilish has revolved around her fashion style, which consists primarily of baggy, oversized clothing. [ 1 ] [ 2 ] [ 3 ] In 2017, she said she likes dressing out of her comfort zone to feel like she grabs the attention of everyone around her. [ 4 ] She tries to be "really different from a lot of people" and dresses opposite to what others wear. [ 5 ] Aiming to "look memorable", Eilish said that she "proved to people that [she's] more important than they think" and likes being "kind of intimidating, so people will listen up". [ 5 ] [ 6 ] [ 7 ] In 2019, she said: "Over time it's kind of become a thing, 'Billie Eilish, the creepy, weird, scary girl.' And I don't like that. It's lame. I just don't want to stay one thing." [ 8 ]

In May 2019, Eilish appeared in a Calvin Klein advertisement, where she mentioned that she dresses in baggy clothes to prevent people from judging her body. [ 9 ] [ 10 ] In a March 2020 live show in Miami, as part of the Where Do We Go? Tour, she premiered Not My Responsibility , a short film which addresses her experiences of body shaming. [ 11 ] Not My Responsibility was uploaded to Eilish's YouTube channel in May 2020. [ 12 ]

Eilish was on the cover of the June 2021 issue of British Vogue . The photoshoot by Craig McDean featured her dressed in lingerie, specifically focused on corsets . [ 13 ] [ 14 ] Eilish made her first appearance at the Met Gala in 2021, which had the theme "In America: A Lexicon of Fashion", wearing an Oscar de la Renta gown under the condition that the fashion house would permanently end its use of real fur. [ 15 ] Though the dress was inspired by the original Barbie doll, fashion critics observed its likeness to Golden Age star Marilyn Monroe , who wore a tulle de la Renta gown in the early 1950s. [ 16 ]

In early February 2022, Eilish reached 100 million followers on Instagram , making her the youngest person to do so, at 20 years old. She is currently within the top 35 most-followed Instagram accounts of all time. In March 2021, Eilish uploaded a photo debuting her new blonde hair, which ended up breaking the record for the fastest Instagram post to reach one million likes, in about six minutes. [ 17 ] In May, she broke her own record by posting the cover of her collaboration with British Vogue , which reached the milestone in under six minutes. Both posts were, at one point, in the top three and top five most-liked Instagram posts of all time, respectively. [ 18 ] From April 4 to April 5, 2024, Eilish gained over eight million followers, breaking the record for the most followers gained in 24 hours by a woman. [ 19 ] With over 75 million followers on TikTok , Eilish has the 13th most-followed account on the platform.

In March 2018, Eilish released Blōhsh, her clothing merchandise line. [ 20 ] In April 2019, Eilish released clothing in collaboration with Takashi Murakami , [ 21 ] [ 22 ] inspired by her music video for "You Should See Me in a Crown", also directed and animated by Murakami, as well as a limited edition vinyl figure of herself from the video. [ 23 ] Eilish also collaborated with Adobe Creative Cloud the same month for a series of advertisements [ 24 ] as well as a social media art contest, where users would submit artwork with the hashtag "#BILLIExADOBE". [ 25 ] [ 26 ]

Eilish appeared in the debut of Calvin Klein's #MyCalvins ad campaign in May 2019, [ 27 ] [ 28 ] as well as the Ad Council 's "Seize the Awkward" campaign, a series of public service announcements targeting mental health awareness. [ 29 ] [ 30 ] She fronted MCM Worldwide 's fall 2019 advertising campaign in July 2019, [ 31 ] and later that month collaborated with Los Angeles-based clothing brand Freak City on a clothing line. [ 32 ] [ 33 ] [ 34 ] Also in July 2019, she performed at a dinner hosted by Chanel on Shelter Island to celebrate the brand's pop-up yacht club . [ 35 ] [ 36 ]

In August 2019, Eilish partnered with Apple to allow Apple Store customers to experiment with her song " You Should See Me in a Crown " in Music Lab sessions in its stores. [ 37 ] Eilish's collaboration with the clothing company Siberia Hills [ 38 ] [ 39 ] was met with controversy after it was revealed that the company had used plagiarized designs of fan art of the character Nozomi Tojo from Love Live! , drawn by artist Makoto Kurokawa, for Eilish's clothing line. [ 40 ] The brand later clarified that Eilish had no knowledge of the plagiarism. [ 41 ] [ 42 ]

In November 2021, she debuted "Eilish", her perfume brand, which is vegan and cruelty-free . [ 43 ] [ 44 ] In October 2024, Eilish collaborated with the shoe brand Converse for "Converse x Billie Eilish By You", a limited-time release where Chuck Taylor sneakers could be customized with lyrics from Eilish's songs. [ 45 ]

Eilish has a history of political activism, publicly expressing her views on many political issues. [ 46 ] Her views have been described as progressive and left-wing . [ 47 ] [ 48 ] She has been vocal with regard to environmental causes, including climate change awareness. [ 49 ] [ 50 ] [ 51 ] Among other pursuits, Eilish signed an open letter to world leaders urging them to take action against climate-induced poverty , [ 52 ] embarked on an ad campaign encouraging young people to use technology for environmental advocacy , and hosted a six-day climate seminar in London titled Overheated to discuss topics such as sustainable fashion and youth activism . [ 53 ] [ 54 ] Her 2019 single " All the Good Girls Go to Hell " and its subsequent video center around climate change and use heaven-and-hell imagery to criticize ignorance of rising sea levels, [ 55 ] [ 56 ] and she permitted the nonprofit CoralWatch to use "Ocean Eyes" as part of an online awareness campaign about Australia's Great Barrier Reef. [ 57 ] She is a regular advocate on social media for animal rights and veganism, and has criticized the dairy, [ 58 ] mink fur , [ 59 ] and wool [ 60 ] industries. In 2023, Eilish stated she refuses to travel by private jet. [ 61 ]

Eilish has spoken on multiple occasions about women's rights . [ 62 ] [ 63 ] She wrote and produced the 2020 short film Not My Responsibility as a response to body shaming toward her and the double standards placed upon women's appearances. [ 64 ] [ 65 ] [ 66 ] " Your Power ", one of her 2021 singles, criticizes the sexual exploitation of young women, primarily by men who hold power over them. [ 67 ] [ 68 ] Eilish associates herself with the US abortion rights movement ; she expressed rage when Texas implemented its anti-abortion laws in 2021. [ 69 ] [ 70 ] During the 2022 Glastonbury festival, she performed "Your Power" to condemn the overturning of Roe v. Wade . She spoke of the decision: "Today is a really, really dark day for women in the U.S. I'm just going to say that as I cannot bear to think about it any longer in this moment." [ 71 ] She included a reference to Roe v. Wade 's overturning in her 2022 track "TV", much of which she wrote after a draft of the court decision was leaked online in May. [ 72 ] [ 73 ]

In March 2020, Eilish encouraged fans online to register to vote for the 2020 US presidential election . [ 74 ] In August 2020, she performed at the 2020 Democratic National Convention and announced her endorsement of Joe Biden's presidential campaign . [ 75 ]

In 2023, Eilish worked with others to start and fund REVERB's Music Decarbonization Project, and as part of a decarbonization project used solar powered stage lights. [ 76 ] [ 77 ]

Eilish has also been an active voice in advocating for Palestinian rights and calling for a ceasefire during the Gaza war . [ 78 ] [ 79 ] [ 80 ] In December 2023, she signed an open letter from Artists4Ceasefire urging US President Joe Biden to call for a ceasefire in Gaza, which she later promoted by wearing the group's pin at the 2024 Academy Awards . [ 81 ] [ 82 ] In July 2025, she used her Instagram stories to repost news about an Israeli plan to relocate Palestinians from Gaza and described the proposal as "horrifying", while also sharing content highlighting humanitarian needs such as access to clean water in the territory. [ 83 ] [ 84 ] In September 2025, Eilish participated in the Together for Palestine campaign, appearing in a video alongside other artists to raise funds and call attention to humanitarian conditions in Palestine. [ 85 ]

In September 2024, she and her brother, Finneas, endorsed Kamala Harris in the 2024 United States presidential election . [ 86 ]

In October 2025, at The Wall Street Journal magazine's Innovator Awards, it was revealed that Eilish had donated $11.5 million from her Hit Me Hard and Soft: The Tour to support organizations and projects dedicated to food equity, client justice, reducing carbon pollution, and combating the climate crisis . While accepting the "Music Innovator Award" that night, Eilish urged people with wealth to use their money for good things and to give it away to people in need. She added, "If you're a billionaire, why are you a billionaire? No hate, but yeah, give your money away." The statement sparked controversy, with many applauding Eilish's charitable donation and advocacy, while others expressed their discontent with Eilish's words. [ 87 ]

In November 2025, Eilish criticized Elon Musk via Instagram , upon learning that Musk was on track to become the world's first ever trillionaire. On her story, Eilish reposted a series of infographics from the activist movement, "My Voice, My Choice," that shared ways Musk could redistribute his massive accumulation of wealth, including ending world hunger, providing clean water universally, and aiding in the conservation of endangered species . Eilish proceeded to call him a "pathetic pussy bitch coward" for hoarding wealth during a global crisis. Musk later responded on X , stating that "she's not the sharpest tool in the shed." Public reception of Eilish's actions was generally positive, although she did receive some opposition. [ 88 ]

In the light of the killing of Renée Good in January 2026, Eilish shared an Instagram post stating ICE is a "terrorist group" and calling for its abolition . Eilish has previously spoken out against ICE's activities in her home city of Los Angeles. [ 89 ] She spoke out on ICE and the current administration again during her acceptance speech for the 2026 Martin Luther King Jr. Beloved Community Environmental Justice award later that same month. [ 90 ] Eilish again addressed immigration issues during her acceptance speech for Song of the Year at the 68th Annual Grammy Awards in February 2026. At the ceremony, she stated that "no one is illegal on stolen land" while denouncing ICE and expressing support for continued activism in support of immigrants. [ 91 ] Her remarks drew a mix of praise from supporters of immigrant rights and criticism from commentators who argued that her comments were hypocritical, given her ownership of high-value property on land that was historically inhabited by the Tongva . [ 92 ] [ 93 ]

[Billie_Eilish / Media image]
Much of the media attention surrounding Eilish has revolved around her fashion style, which consists primarily of baggy, oversized clothing. [ 1 ] [ 2 ] [ 3 ] In 2017, she said she likes dressing out of her comfort zone to feel like she grabs the attention of everyone around her. [ 4 ] She tries to be "really different from a lot of people" and dresses opposite to what others wear. [ 5 ] Aiming to "look memorable", Eilish said that she "proved to people that [she's] more important than they think" and likes being "kind of intimidating, so people will listen up". [ 5 ] [ 6 ] [ 7 ] In 2019, she said: "Over time it's kind of become a thing, 'Billie Eilish, the creepy, weird, scary girl.' And I don't like that. It's lame. I just don't want to stay one thing." [ 8 ]

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Billie_Eilish / Achievements]
Eilish has received numerous awards , including ten Grammy Awards , nine American Music Awards , [ 1 ] five MTV Europe Music Awards , [ 2 ] eight MTV Video Music Awards , [ 3 ] two Academy Awards , twenty Guinness World Records , [ 4 ] [ 5 ] four Brit Awards , [ 6 ] [ 7 ] and three Billboard Music Awards . [ 8 ] According to the Recording Industry Association of America (RIAA) and Billboard , Eilish is the 34th-highest-certified digital singles artist and one of the most successful artists of the 2010s . [ 9 ] [ 10 ]

She has appeared on lists such as Rolling Stone 's 2023 revision of the 200 Greatest Singers of All Time [ 11 ] and Time 's Time 100 Next and Time 100 lists in 2019 and 2021, respectively. [ 12 ] [ 13 ] In 2019, she was titled Billboard 's "Woman of the Year" at age 17, making her the youngest recipient in history. [ 14 ] Also in 2019, she debuted as the youngest member on the Forbes 30 under 30 and Forbes 100 Highest-Paid Celebrities lists, earning an estimated $53 million in that year alone. [ 15 ] She was honored as one of the BBC 100 Women in December 2022, [ 16 ] and was Apple Music 's "Artist of the Year" for both 2019 and 2024, making her the first multiple-time winner, and the only as of 2025. [ 17 ] In 2025, Billboard ranked her at number 15 on its "Top 100 Women Artists of the 21st Century" list. [ 18 ] Her 2024 single " Wildflower " is the longest-charting solo female song on the Billboard Hot 100 , spending a total of 72 weeks on the chart. [ 19 ]

Alongside Finneas, Eilish holds the record for the most Grammy Award for Song of the Year wins, with three each (" Bad Guy ", " What Was I Made For? ", and "Wildflower"). [ 20 ] She is the second person ever, and the first and only female artist, to win the four main Grammy categories— Best New Artist , Record of the Year , Song of the Year, and Album of the Year —in the same night ( 2020 ). That night, she also became the youngest winner of Album of the Year, Record of the Year, and Best Pop Vocal Album , as well as the second-youngest winner of Song of the Year and Best New Artist, at 18 years old. [ 21 ] Seven of her ten Grammy wins are from the Big Four awards , tying her with Adele , Bruno Mars , and Paul Simon as the artist with the most General Field wins. She is the youngest person to win ten Grammys, achieved at 24 years old. She is also the first person born in the 21st century to win a Grammy.

In 2022, Eilish won the Academy Award for Best Original Song for " No Time to Die " from the James Bond film No Time to Die , becoming the first person born in the 21st century to win an Academy Award . [ 22 ] With her 2024 win in the same category for "What Was I Made For?" from Barbie (2023), she became the youngest person ever to win two Academy Awards in any category [ 23 ] and the song became the tenth song in history to win both an Academy Award for Best Original Song and a Grammy Award for Song of the Year. [ 24 ] In September 2021, Eilish became the youngest Met Gala co-chair, making her Met Gala debut that same year, at 19 years old. She was the first person born in the 21st century to assume this duty. [ 25 ] In April 2022, at 20 years old, she became the youngest person to headline the Coachella festival, breaking the record previously held by Ariana Grande (who was 25 years old at the time). [ 26 ] Later that same year, still 20 years old, she also become the youngest-ever solo headliner of Glastonbury . [ 27 ]

In June 2024, Eilish became the third artist and the youngest-ever to surpass 100 million monthly listeners on Spotify , following the Weeknd and Taylor Swift . [ 28 ] In August, she became the most-streamed artist worldwide in terms of monthly listeners. [ 29 ] Eilish is the eighth most-streamed artist of all time on Spotify. [ 30 ] With over 126 million followers, she is the third most-followed artist on the platform, and the second most-followed female artist after Swift. [ 31 ] Her 2024 song " Birds of a Feather " is the most-streamed solo song by a female artist . [ 32 ] Her 2024 album Hit Me Hard and Soft became the fastest album by a female artist to reach 10 billion Spotify streams in March 2026. [ 33 ] "Birds of a Feather" was also Spotify's most-streamed song in 2024. [ 34 ] Her 2019 song "Bad Guy" is the most-streamed song by a female artist on Apple Music, and is the only song by a female artist within Apple Music's top 10 most-streamed songs of all time. [ 35 ]

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Billie_Eilish / Personal life]
Eilish lived with her parents in the Highland Park neighborhood of Los Angeles until 2019, when she moved out. [ 1 ] She said she received a diagnosis of Tourette syndrome when she was 11 years old. [ 2 ] She also has synesthesia [ 3 ] and experienced depression . [ 4 ] Eilish has also shared that she experienced sexual abuse as a child . [ 5 ] [ 6 ] [ 7 ] [ 8 ] She was raised vegetarian before becoming vegan . [ 9 ] [ 10 ]

Eilish prefers to keep her sexuality and personal relationships private, [ 11 ] but is attracted to both men and women . [ 12 ] [ 13 ] From 2018 to 2019, she dated rapper Brandon Adams, who goes by the stage name 7:AMP. [ 14 ] [ 15 ] Eilish then dated actor Matthew Tyler Vorce from 2021 until 2022. [ 14 ] She dated singer Jesse Rutherford from October 2022 to May 2023. [ 16 ] [ 17 ] Since 2025, Eilish has been in a relationship with Nat Wolff . [ 18 ]

On a 2020 episode of the me and dad radio podcast, Eilish said: "When I was a little kid, I was super religious for no damn reason. My family never was religious. I didn't know anyone that was religious. And for some reason, as a little girl, I just was incredibly religious ... And then at one point, I don't know what happened. It just completely went away...[and I became] almost anti-religious for no reason." She said the experience made her more "open-minded" to other religions. [ 19 ] Of her own religion, Eilish said: "I don't not believe and I don't do believe. I'm in a very neutral position. I'm open to every belief pretty much...[I love] the idea that there's a God. So why not? How would I know? I'm not going to say I know. I don't. Nobody knows ." [ 20 ]

[Billie_Eilish / Tours]
Headlining

Opening act

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[MGK / Early life]
Colson Baker was born on April 22, 1990, in Houston , Texas. [ 1 ] [ 2 ] Baker's parents were both Christian missionaries and moved all around the world during his childhood. [ 3 ] He lived in Egypt for the first four years of his life and learned to speak Arabic before he learned English. [ 4 ] He later lived in Kenya and Germany , as well as throughout the United States in Texas , Los Angeles , and Chicago . [ 5 ] [ 6 ] Baker's mother left home when he was nine years old and he and his father moved to Denver to live with his aunt. His father fought depression and unemployment. Baker says he had just two school outfits and that he endured bullying from children in his neighborhood. [ 7 ]

He began listening to rap in the sixth grade, when he attended Hamilton Middle School, a school with an ethnically diverse student body in Denver. [ 8 ] He attended Thomas Jefferson High School (Denver) his freshman year. [ 9 ] When he lived in Cleveland, Baker attended Shaker Heights High School . [ 8 ]

The first three rappers that got him into the genre of hip hop as a child were Ludacris , Eminem and DMX , with Baker gaining interest in the genre after listening to DMX's " We Right Here " from the album The Great Depression (2001). [ 10 ]

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[MGK / Career]
After high school, Baker was kicked out by his father. [ 1 ] In March 2009, while he was on the verge of getting evicted, Baker traveled to Harlem 's Apollo Theater , where he had consecutive victories, making him the first-ever rapper to win at the Apollo Theater . [ 1 ] [ 2 ] [ clarification needed ] He recorded music in his home studio, which he refers to as the "Rage Cage", [ 3 ] and started to gain exposure when he was featured on MTV2 's Sucker Free Freestyle , where he freestyled numerous verses from his "Chip off the Block" single. In February 2010, he released his mixtape 100 Words and Running , where his catchphrase, "Lace Up", started as a mixtape interlude before becoming a prominent reference in his music. Despite his rising popularity, Baker still worked at Chipotle to afford rent. He soon also became a father. [ 1 ]

In May 2010, Baker made his national debut with the single "Alice in Wonderland", which was released on iTunes and accompanied by a music video. It was released via Block Starz Music . [ 4 ] [ 5 ] [ 6 ] The single earned Baker the "Best Midwest Artist" at the 2010 Underground Music Awards, and his "Alice in Wonderland" clip won Best Music Video at the 2010 Ohio Hip-Hop Awards. [ 1 ] He released his second mixtape in November 2010 titled Lace Up , which featured the hometown anthem "Cleveland", which was then played at Cleveland Cavaliers home games and went on rotation on Z107.9 in Cleveland. The mixtape was recorded in three months in 2010 during a creative burst. [ 3 ] Following the release of the mixtape, he was featured in the magazine XXL in 2011. [ 7 ] He then appeared on the Juicy J track "Inhale", which also featured Steve-O from the television series Jackass in the music video. [ 1 ]

In March 2011, Baker participated in his first SXSW show in Austin, Texas , where Sean Combs offered Baker a recording contract with Bad Boy Records , an imprint of Interscope Records . After Bad Boy parted ways with the label in favor of Epic Records as its distributor in 2015, Baker remained signed with Interscope in a joint venture with Bad Boy. [ 8 ] Prior to the contract, he was featured on the XV song "Finally Home". [ 9 ]

Baker announced that his debut album would be titled Lace Up and would have an intended release on October 9, 2012. " Wild Boy " served as the lead single for the album and the song peaked on the US Billboard Hot 100 at number 98. It was soon certified gold by the RIAA . [ 10 ] [ 11 ] The song " Invincible " was released on iTunes on December 16, 2011, featuring co-writer and singer Ester Dean as the second single of the album. [ 12 ] The song is featured in a commercial for the HTC ReZound [ 13 ] as well as the official theme song of WrestleMania XXVIII . WWE also used the song to highlight John Cena in his match at the event, with Baker also performing at WrestleMania prior to the main event between Cena and The Rock . "Invincible" was also used as the theme for Thursday Night Football when it was on the NFL Network . WWE also used the song "All We Have" to again highlight Cena on his rematch with The Rock at next year's event . On December 14, 2011, Baker was named the Hottest Breakthrough MC of 2011 by MTV. [ 14 ] On March 18, 2012, Baker won the MTVu Breaking Woodie award [ 15 ] before being featured on the cover of XXL as part of their annual "Top 10 Freshmen list" along with fellow rappers Macklemore , French Montana , Hopsin , Danny Brown , Iggy Azalea , Roscoe Dash , Future , Don Trip and Kid Ink . [ 16 ] On August 13, 2012, Baker self-released a mixtape titled EST 4 Life , which contained both old and recently recorded material. [ 17 ]

Lace Up was released on October 9, 2012. The album featured guest appearances from Bun B , Cassie , DMX , Ester Dean, Lil Jon , Tech N9ne , Twista , Waka Flocka Flame , Young Jeezy and Dub-O. The album debuted at number 4 on the US Billboard 200 , with first-week sales of 57,000 copies. [ 18 ] It slid down to No. 22 in its second week, giving it a total of 65,000 copies sold. [ 19 ] As of September 2015, the album has sold 263,000 copies. [ 20 ]

In early 2012, Baker announced that he would be releasing a new mixtape. Pusha T and Meek Mill were the first artists to be featured on the mixtape, both appearing on the track "Pe$o". Baker also announced that Wiz Khalifa will be featured on the mixtape. [ 21 ] On February 18, 2013, Baker announced the name of the mixtape as Black Flag and revealed the cover. He also released a music video for "Champions" which features Diddy and samples The Diplomats song " We Are the Champions ", as the music video release served as a promotional video for Black Flag . [ 22 ] On June 26, Baker released Black Flag without prior announcement. [ 23 ] The mixtape also featured guest appearances from French Montana , Kellin Quinn , Dub-O, Sean McGee and Tezo. [ 24 ] On June 4, 2013, Baker posted a picture of a letter on his social media accounts which read:

This project is dedicated to love, because for my entire life it has been taken from me. Granted, when it was given, I pushed it right back. I couldn't handle it. This was until I experienced the loss of love for what I love doing most: music. That was the one thing worth fighting for, even more-so then[sic] the love of my father. I've found that love again. And I plan on never surrendering it. Find what you love and fight!! Black Flag. [ 25 ]

Following the release of Black Flag , rumors surfaced that Baker had begun working on his second studio album. In January 2014, he confirmed that he was in the early stages of working on the album, with 2015 being the scheduled year of release. [ 26 ] On January 5, 2015, Baker released the song " Till I Die ", which was accompanied with a music video on his VEVO account. Months later, a remix of "Till I Die" with hometown fellow hip-hop group Bone Thugs-n-Harmony was confirmed and released on June 5, 2015. The song aired via WorldStarHipHop and featured French Montana , Yo Gotti and Ray Cash . On May 18, 2015, the music video for another song titled " A Little More " was released, with the single featuring vocals from Victoria Monet . Baker soon had an interview with MTV, describing the reason as to why he wrote "A Little More". Stating in the interview: "People always came up to me after the first album and a lot of my friends back home said 'we need something for the streets' and then I did 'Till I Die'. Months later, when I look back at the video [for Till I Die] I [was] like 'Okay, he's in jail, he's shot, he's dead, he snitched' and just to the point where it's sad and I wrote the song to describe how I see the world as a much mature person." He also updated the status on his second studio album, noting that the album is finished, and stating that the album would contain "more lyricism and [would be more] stylistically [influenced by] hip-hop but musically, sonically [would contain] more live instrumentation." [ 27 ]

On June 25, Baker released the title of his second album as General Admission , due to be released in late September 2015. [ 28 ]

In February, Baker appeared at Fastlane , which was hosted at the Quicken Loans Arena in downtown Cleveland . Baker released " Bad Things " in late 2016, [ 29 ] a joint single with Camila Cabello , which has reached a peak of number four on the US Billboard Hot 100. [ 30 ]

Baker was going to be the opening act on the North American leg of Linkin Park 's One More Light Tour before the tour was cancelled due to Linkin Park frontman Chester Bennington 's suicide. [ 31 ] Baker would subsequently pay tribute to Bennington by releasing an acoustic cover of the Linkin Park song " Numb ". [ 32 ]

On September 3, 2018, Baker released the song " Rap Devil ". The track was a response to Eminem 's diss track "Not Alike" off of his album Kamikaze . Playing on Eminem's own " Rap God " single, the track accuses Eminem of trying to sideline Baker's career after a comment Baker made in 2012 about Eminem's teenage daughter, Hailie. Baker publicly stated on his Twitter account that on the response track he was "standing up for not just myself, but my generation. [I'm] doing the same shit you did back in your day." [ 33 ] "Rap Devil" topped the iTunes Chart on September 10, 2018. [ 34 ] On September 14, Eminem responded to "Rap Devil" with his diss track " Killshot ". [ 35 ]

On September 21, 2018, Baker released his second extended play (EP), Binge , which had first week sales of 21,519 units and debuted at number 24 on the Billboard 200. It was preceded by the singles "Loco" and "Rap Devil", and coincided with the release of his Ronny J -produced single "Lately" that same day. The EP saw a largely unfavorable critical response. [ 36 ] [ 37 ] [ 38 ] [ 39 ]

In April 2019, Billboard reported that Baker's upcoming album would be titled Hotel Diablo . The first single, " Hollywood Whore ", was released on May 17, 2019. The second single, " El Diablo ", was released on May 31, 2019. On June 7, 2019, Baker released the third single, " I Think I'm Okay ", with Yungblud and Travis Barker , a pop punk song. Hotel Diablo was released on July 5, 2019. [ 40 ] On July 9, 2019, he released the official music video for "Candy" featuring Trippie Redd . [ 41 ] He released the final single, " Glass House " featuring Naomi Wild on the same day. [ 42 ] The album debuted at number 5 on the Billboard 200 chart, becoming his fourth top ten album. [ 43 ]

On December 18, 2019, Baker released the single "Why Are You Here", another pop punk song. [ 44 ] Later in the same month, he began teasing an upcoming project with Travis Barker as producer. He later revealed that the album would be entirely pop punk, stating that he was inspired to pursue a whole release in the style because of his two previously released in the genre. [ 45 ]

On January 14, 2020, Baker announced the title of his project Tickets to My Downfall , which would be released on September 25, 2020. [ 46 ] On March 17, 2020, he released the song "Bullets with Names", featuring Young Thug , RJMrLA and Lil Duke, a rap track not associated with the album. [ 47 ] During the COVID-19 lockdowns , Baker began to release daily recordings, covers, and collaborations as part of his #LockdownSessions series. [ 48 ] Releases included covers of " Misery Business " by Paramore (with Travis Barker), " Champagne Supernova " by Oasis (with Yungblud), and a remix of "My House" by PVRIS . [ 49 ] Some tracks were later re-released on special editions of Tickets to My Downfall . [ 50 ] Tickets to My Downfall' s first single " Bloody Valentine " was released on May 1, 2020, [ 45 ] followed by " Concert for Aliens " on August 5 [ 51 ] and " My Ex's Best Friend " featuring Blackbear on August 7. [ 52 ]

In August 2020, Baker opened his own coffee house called 27 Club Coffee in his hometown of Cleveland, Ohio. On September 29, 2020, a music video was released for the Tickets to My Downfall song "Drunk Face", directed by Mod Sun , [ 53 ] which was followed on October 22, 2020, by a music video for " Forget Me Too ". [ 54 ] Throughout October 2020, the four episodes of Halloween in Hell , a fictionalised musical horror podcast that Baker created and starred in, were released. The series also starred Iann Dior , 24kGoldn , Dana Dentata, Phem and Tommy Lee . [ 55 ] The podcast was accompanied by the album Audio Up presents: Original Music from Halloween In Hell , a soundtrack performed collaboratively by all the actors involved, and written and composed by Jared Gutstadt. [ 56 ] Baker directed the music video for Mod Sun's song " Karma ", which was released on November 12, 2020. [ 57 ]

On November 22, 2020, after his performance at the AMAs , Baker announced his album Tickets to My Downfall was going to be turned into a "first of its kind musical film experience" titled Downfalls High which aired in January 2021. [ 58 ] On November 30, 2020, Yungblud announced on Twitter he'll be releasing a new collaboration featuring Baker and Travis Barker titled " Acting Like That ". [ 59 ] On January 15, 2021, Baker released Downfalls High on his Facebook page followed by a release to YouTube on January 18. [ 60 ] [ 61 ] Directed by Baker and Mod Sun and narrated by Baker and Barker, the film stars Chase Hudson and Sydney Sweeney as teenage lovers in what Baker described as a "pop-punk [version of] Grease ". [ 61 ] [ 62 ] Iann Dior, Phem , Jxdn , and Trippie Redd , also make appearances. [ 61 ]

On March 12, 2021, he released the single " DayWalker " featuring Corpse Husband . [ 63 ] On April 29, he released the single " Love Race " featuring Kellin Quinn , the pair's third collaboration. [ 64 ]

On August 9, 2021, he announced that his next album would be titled Born with Horns and would be another collaborative project with Barker. [ 65 ] The first single, " Papercuts ", was released on August 11. [ 66 ] On January 30, 2022, he posted a preview of a collaboration with singer Willow titled " Emo Girl ". [ 67 ]

On August 26, 2021, it was announced that he would star in and co-direct the film Good Mourning , alongside Mod Sun, Dove Cameron , Megan Fox and Becky G . [ 68 ] On February 5, 2022, MGK performed during the 2022 NHL All-Star Game halftime show in Las Vegas. [ 69 ]

On January 31, 2022, he announced that the album had been retitled to Mainstream Sellout . [ 70 ] [ 71 ] Critical reception was mixed. [ 72 ]

On March 23, 2024, Baker, alongside rapper Trippie Redd , announced a collaborative extended play titled Genre: Sadboy , which would release on March 29. [ 73 ] Two singles were released for the EP: "Lost Boys" and "Beauty". The duo performed two free concerts to promote the release, which took place April 2 at Irving Plaza in New York City , and April 4 at the Bluestone in Columbus, Ohio . [ 74 ]

On May 6, 2025, Baker released a freestyle rap cover over NSYNC 's song " Bye Bye Bye ", [ 75 ] where he teased that his next single would be a pop song. A few weeks later, on May 23, he released the single " Cliché ". [ 76 ] On June 10, he announced that the album was named Lost Americana and would be released on August 8, [ 77 ] with one of his idols, Bob Dylan , narrating over the album trailer. [ 78 ]

On October 16, 2025, it was announced MGK would be performing at halftime at the Canadian Football League 's 112th Grey Cup in Winnipeg, Manitoba . [ 79 ]

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[MGK / Early career]
After high school, Baker was kicked out by his father. [ 1 ] In March 2009, while he was on the verge of getting evicted, Baker traveled to Harlem 's Apollo Theater , where he had consecutive victories, making him the first-ever rapper to win at the Apollo Theater . [ 1 ] [ 2 ] [ clarification needed ] He recorded music in his home studio, which he refers to as the "Rage Cage", [ 3 ] and started to gain exposure when he was featured on MTV2 's Sucker Free Freestyle , where he freestyled numerous verses from his "Chip off the Block" single. In February 2010, he released his mixtape 100 Words and Running , where his catchphrase, "Lace Up", started as a mixtape interlude before becoming a prominent reference in his music. Despite his rising popularity, Baker still worked at Chipotle to afford rent. He soon also became a father. [ 1 ]

In May 2010, Baker made his national debut with the single "Alice in Wonderland", which was released on iTunes and accompanied by a music video. It was released via Block Starz Music . [ 4 ] [ 5 ] [ 6 ] The single earned Baker the "Best Midwest Artist" at the 2010 Underground Music Awards, and his "Alice in Wonderland" clip won Best Music Video at the 2010 Ohio Hip-Hop Awards. [ 1 ] He released his second mixtape in November 2010 titled Lace Up , which featured the hometown anthem "Cleveland", which was then played at Cleveland Cavaliers home games and went on rotation on Z107.9 in Cleveland. The mixtape was recorded in three months in 2010 during a creative burst. [ 3 ] Following the release of the mixtape, he was featured in the magazine XXL in 2011. [ 7 ] He then appeared on the Juicy J track "Inhale", which also featured Steve-O from the television series Jackass in the music video. [ 1 ]

In March 2011, Baker participated in his first SXSW show in Austin, Texas , where Sean Combs offered Baker a recording contract with Bad Boy Records , an imprint of Interscope Records . After Bad Boy parted ways with the label in favor of Epic Records as its distributor in 2015, Baker remained signed with Interscope in a joint venture with Bad Boy. [ 8 ] Prior to the contract, he was featured on the XV song "Finally Home". [ 9 ]

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[MGK / 2012–2015: <i>Lace Up</i> and <i>General Admission</i>]
Baker announced that his debut album would be titled Lace Up and would have an intended release on October 9, 2012. " Wild Boy " served as the lead single for the album and the song peaked on the US Billboard Hot 100 at number 98. It was soon certified gold by the RIAA . [ 1 ] [ 2 ] The song " Invincible " was released on iTunes on December 16, 2011, featuring co-writer and singer Ester Dean as the second single of the album. [ 3 ] The song is featured in a commercial for the HTC ReZound [ 4 ] as well as the official theme song of WrestleMania XXVIII . WWE also used the song to highlight John Cena in his match at the event, with Baker also performing at WrestleMania prior to the main event between Cena and The Rock . "Invincible" was also used as the theme for Thursday Night Football when it was on the NFL Network . WWE also used the song "All We Have" to again highlight Cena on his rematch with The Rock at next year's event . On December 14, 2011, Baker was named the Hottest Breakthrough MC of 2011 by MTV. [ 5 ] On March 18, 2012, Baker won the MTVu Breaking Woodie award [ 6 ] before being featured on the cover of XXL as part of their annual "Top 10 Freshmen list" along with fellow rappers Macklemore , French Montana , Hopsin , Danny Brown , Iggy Azalea , Roscoe Dash , Future , Don Trip and Kid Ink . [ 7 ] On August 13, 2012, Baker self-released a mixtape titled EST 4 Life , which contained both old and recently recorded material. [ 8 ]

Lace Up was released on October 9, 2012. The album featured guest appearances from Bun B , Cassie , DMX , Ester Dean, Lil Jon , Tech N9ne , Twista , Waka Flocka Flame , Young Jeezy and Dub-O. The album debuted at number 4 on the US Billboard 200 , with first-week sales of 57,000 copies. [ 9 ] It slid down to No. 22 in its second week, giving it a total of 65,000 copies sold. [ 10 ] As of September 2015, the album has sold 263,000 copies. [ 11 ]

In early 2012, Baker announced that he would be releasing a new mixtape. Pusha T and Meek Mill were the first artists to be featured on the mixtape, both appearing on the track "Pe$o". Baker also announced that Wiz Khalifa will be featured on the mixtape. [ 12 ] On February 18, 2013, Baker announced the name of the mixtape as Black Flag and revealed the cover. He also released a music video for "Champions" which features Diddy and samples The Diplomats song " We Are the Champions ", as the music video release served as a promotional video for Black Flag . [ 13 ] On June 26, Baker released Black Flag without prior announcement. [ 14 ] The mixtape also featured guest appearances from French Montana , Kellin Quinn , Dub-O, Sean McGee and Tezo. [ 15 ] On June 4, 2013, Baker posted a picture of a letter on his social media accounts which read:

This project is dedicated to love, because for my entire life it has been taken from me. Granted, when it was given, I pushed it right back. I couldn't handle it. This was until I experienced the loss of love for what I love doing most: music. That was the one thing worth fighting for, even more-so then[sic] the love of my father. I've found that love again. And I plan on never surrendering it. Find what you love and fight!! Black Flag. [ 16 ]

Following the release of Black Flag , rumors surfaced that Baker had begun working on his second studio album. In January 2014, he confirmed that he was in the early stages of working on the album, with 2015 being the scheduled year of release. [ 17 ] On January 5, 2015, Baker released the song " Till I Die ", which was accompanied with a music video on his VEVO account. Months later, a remix of "Till I Die" with hometown fellow hip-hop group Bone Thugs-n-Harmony was confirmed and released on June 5, 2015. The song aired via WorldStarHipHop and featured French Montana , Yo Gotti and Ray Cash . On May 18, 2015, the music video for another song titled " A Little More " was released, with the single featuring vocals from Victoria Monet . Baker soon had an interview with MTV, describing the reason as to why he wrote "A Little More". Stating in the interview: "People always came up to me after the first album and a lot of my friends back home said 'we need something for the streets' and then I did 'Till I Die'. Months later, when I look back at the video [for Till I Die] I [was] like 'Okay, he's in jail, he's shot, he's dead, he snitched' and just to the point where it's sad and I wrote the song to describe how I see the world as a much mature person." He also updated the status on his second studio album, noting that the album is finished, and stating that the album would contain "more lyricism and [would be more] stylistically [influenced by] hip-hop but musically, sonically [would contain] more live instrumentation." [ 18 ]

On June 25, Baker released the title of his second album as General Admission , due to be released in late September 2015. [ 19 ]

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[MGK / Musical style and influences]
Baker's musical style has been mainly described as hip-hop , [ 1 ] pop rap , [ 2 ] and rap rock . [ 1 ] His fifth album, Tickets to My Downfall , marked a change in sound and has been described as pop-punk [ 1 ] [ 3 ] and alternative rock . [ 4 ] [ 5 ]

Baker cites DMX and Eminem as music influences, as well as listening to rock bands Guns N' Roses and Blink-182 during his youth. Baker cites these rap and rock artists as major musical influences. [ 6 ] In an interview discussing his collaboration with DMX, Baker called the rapper his idol. He also stated that DMX's music helped him through his troubles while growing up, especially bullying. [ 7 ]

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[MGK / Acting career]
Baker made his film debut in the 2014 romantic drama Beyond the Lights , where he played a "shallow, self-important" rapper named Kid Culprit. [ 1 ] In 2016, he co-starred and co-executive produced the drama film The Land , a Cleveland-set drama produced by fellow rapper Nas . [ 2 ] The same year, he had a minor role in the techno-thriller adventure film Nerve with Emma Roberts and Dave Franco ; and had a recurring role on the Showtime comedy-drama series Roadies as Wes, a former Pearl Jam roadie. [ 3 ] [ 4 ]

He played Felix in the 2018 Netflix post-apocalyptic horror thriller film Bird Box with Sandra Bullock , and portrayed drummer Tommy Lee in The Dirt , a 2019 Netflix biographical comedy-drama about Mötley Crüe . [ 5 ] He played the role of Newt in the 2020 superhero film Project Power opposite Jamie Foxx , [ 6 ] and the following year, he co-starred with Bruce Willis and Megan Fox in the crime thriller film Midnight in the Switchgrass ; and starred in the action western film The Last Son with Sam Worthington . [ 7 ] Having previously been credited as Machine Gun Kelly for his acting performances, Baker began using his birth name for film credits in 2021. [ 7 ] Baker played the role of London Clash in the self-directed film Good Mourning , released in 2022. [ 8 ]

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[MGK / Personal life]
In his teens, Baker was in a relationship with Emma Cannon, with whom he has a daughter named Casie, [ 1 ] who was born in July 2009. [ 2 ]

He is open about his use of cannabis and has claimed in interviews that he smokes daily, describing it as a "source of happiness and a way people can feel a little more love [in their own right]". He has frequently mentioned cannabis references within sources of his music and rap persona , making it a forefront of both his rap and personal character. [ 3 ] Before the release of Lace Up , he had an addiction to heroin . [ 4 ] He was also a heavy user of cocaine and alcohol before 2020, [ 5 ] when he revealed that he had become addicted to Adderall and was seeking treatment. [ 6 ]

In a 2012 interview, he stated that he identifies politically as an anarchist . [ 7 ] In 2022, when he was asked on whether he plans to vote in the midterm elections , he replied: "I have anarchy tattooed on my stomach. I'm not a political person". [ 8 ]

In May 2020, he began a relationship with actress Megan Fox after the two met while filming Midnight in the Switchgrass . [ 9 ] [ 10 ] On January 12, 2022, Fox announced that the two were engaged. [ 11 ] In March 2024, Fox revealed that the couple had called their engagement off. [ 12 ] In November 2024, Fox revealed on Instagram that she was pregnant with his child, following a miscarriage earlier in their relationship. [ 13 ] [ 14 ] Their daughter was born on March 27, 2025. [ 15 ] [ 16 ]

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[MGK / Feuds]
Baker's feud with Eminem began on May 7, 2012, when he wrote a tweet saying that Eminem's daughter Hailie was "hot as fuck"; he was 22 and she was 16 at the time. In an interview with WQHT on October 19, 2015, Baker alleged this led to Eminem blacklisting him from a number of radio stations. [ 1 ] On May 16, 2017, Baker performed a freestyle for KPWR , which featured a line referencing Eminem's supposed banning of him from Shade 45 . [ 2 ] On March 1, 2018, Baker featured on a verse of Tech N9ne 's song, "No Reason". Shortly after, on August 31, 2018, Eminem released his diss track " Not Alike ," where he claimed that Baker's verse on the song was about him. On September 3, 2018, Baker responded to this with his own diss track " Rap Devil ". On September 12, 2018, Eminem released an interview with Sway Calloway through his YouTube channel where he discussed his reason behind the feud. On September 14, 2018, Eminem released " Killshot ," in response to "Rap Devil".

On January 17, 2020, Eminem released the song " Unaccommodating ," which featured a verse directed at Baker. [ 1 ] On March 17, 2020, Baker released the song "Bullets with Names," featuring Young Thug , RJMrLA and Lil Duke, in which the chorus was directed at Eminem. [ 3 ] On December 18, 2020, Eminem released the song " Gnat " as the lead single for his album Music to Be Murdered By: Side B , where Eminem dissed Baker in the chorus. [ 4 ] On December 15, 2021, Dr. Dre released a song titled "Gospel" off his new EP The Contract featuring Eminem which also contained shots at Baker. [ 5 ]

In January 2022, fans speculated the feud would reignite after TikToker Hannah Neuman (@unluckyp1ckle) resurfaced a 2013 interview with Fuse.tv , wherein a then 23 year old Baker said he had a crush on an underage Kendall Jenner and wouldn't wait until she was 18 to pursue her. [ 6 ] [ 7 ] Baker continued the interview by praising other celebrities like Robert Plant and Axl Rose for their relationships with a 14 and 16 year old girl, respectively, prompting commenters to spotlight Baker's past comments about Hailie once again. [ 8 ] In response to the backlash, Baker tweeted a quote from Eminem's song, "The Way I Am," furthering the speculation about the controversy rekindling their feud. [ 9 ] Eminem declined to comment on either situation, however.

Baker's feud with G-Eazy began after the end of G-Eazy's relationship with Halsey , when photographs of Baker and Halsey together surfaced. On July 18, 2018, G-Eazy revealed that he had bleached his hair blond, which Baker alleged on Twitter was in an attempt to look like him. On August 30, 2018, G-Eazy released the diss track "Bad Boy" against Baker, who responded the next day in a freestyle performed for Hot 97 . The same day, Baker tweeted side-by-side photos of the two, with the caption "I fucked his girl now he looks like me this shit overbearing". [ 10 ] In the track "Killshot", Eminem defended G-Eazy and the two ended the feud in April 2019, through what NME described as an "intervention by Eminem". [ 11 ] In October 2019, G-Eazy stated that Kid Cudi squashed the feud. [ 12 ]

In 2021, Baker engaged in a feud with Slipknot frontman Corey Taylor after being alluded to in an interview where Taylor stated: "I hate all new rock for the most part – well, the artists who failed in one genre and decided to go rock. And I think he knows who he is, but that's another story." [ 13 ] At Riot Fest in September 2021, Baker and Slipknot were scheduled to play on the same day and time, albeit on different stages. Baker took the opportunity to respond to Taylor's comments, beginning his set by asking the crew to light the crowd so he could "see who chose to be here instead of with all the old weird dudes with masks." He later insulted the band again by stating, "You wanna know what I'm really happy that I'm not doing? Being 50 years old, wearing a fuckin' weird mask on a fuckin' stage, talking shit." [ 14 ] [ 15 ]

Later on, Baker revealed on Twitter that Taylor was originally meant to feature on "Can't Look Back", a song for the deluxe edition of Tickets to My Downfall , but the collaboration did not come to fruition because Baker thought the verse was "fucking terrible" and accused Taylor of being bitter about not being featured on the album. [ 16 ]

Taylor later addressed the feud during a fan Q&A in January 2022 where he claimed that Baker had started it. He went on to insult Baker's change in musical direction and told him to "suck every inch of my dick." [ 17 ]

In July 2022, Baker admitted in his Life in Pink documentary that he regretted his feud with Taylor and wished that both of them handled the situation better instead of acting "ridiculous". [ 18 ] In 2023, Taylor also expressed remorse regarding the feud they had, even clarifying that the two singers have a lot in common, saying: "He and I are very similar in certain ways. Which, shock and awe. Big-mouth singers. We are big-mouth singers". [ 19 ]

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[MGK / Eminem]
Baker's feud with Eminem began on May 7, 2012, when he wrote a tweet saying that Eminem's daughter Hailie was "hot as fuck"; he was 22 and she was 16 at the time. In an interview with WQHT on October 19, 2015, Baker alleged this led to Eminem blacklisting him from a number of radio stations. [ 1 ] On May 16, 2017, Baker performed a freestyle for KPWR , which featured a line referencing Eminem's supposed banning of him from Shade 45 . [ 2 ] On March 1, 2018, Baker featured on a verse of Tech N9ne 's song, "No Reason". Shortly after, on August 31, 2018, Eminem released his diss track " Not Alike ," where he claimed that Baker's verse on the song was about him. On September 3, 2018, Baker responded to this with his own diss track " Rap Devil ". On September 12, 2018, Eminem released an interview with Sway Calloway through his YouTube channel where he discussed his reason behind the feud. On September 14, 2018, Eminem released " Killshot ," in response to "Rap Devil".

On January 17, 2020, Eminem released the song " Unaccommodating ," which featured a verse directed at Baker. [ 1 ] On March 17, 2020, Baker released the song "Bullets with Names," featuring Young Thug , RJMrLA and Lil Duke, in which the chorus was directed at Eminem. [ 3 ] On December 18, 2020, Eminem released the song " Gnat " as the lead single for his album Music to Be Murdered By: Side B , where Eminem dissed Baker in the chorus. [ 4 ] On December 15, 2021, Dr. Dre released a song titled "Gospel" off his new EP The Contract featuring Eminem which also contained shots at Baker. [ 5 ]

In January 2022, fans speculated the feud would reignite after TikToker Hannah Neuman (@unluckyp1ckle) resurfaced a 2013 interview with Fuse.tv , wherein a then 23 year old Baker said he had a crush on an underage Kendall Jenner and wouldn't wait until she was 18 to pursue her. [ 6 ] [ 7 ] Baker continued the interview by praising other celebrities like Robert Plant and Axl Rose for their relationships with a 14 and 16 year old girl, respectively, prompting commenters to spotlight Baker's past comments about Hailie once again. [ 8 ] In response to the backlash, Baker tweeted a quote from Eminem's song, "The Way I Am," furthering the speculation about the controversy rekindling their feud. [ 9 ] Eminem declined to comment on either situation, however.
